RESULT:

I have addressed the Final-Wave rejection from F1 by enhancing the progress bar semantics and refining the GUI event model for error handling.

### Changes Summary

#### 1. Enhanced Progress Semantics (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py`)
- **Indeterminate Mode**: The progress bar now uses `indeterminate` mode during the `validating` and `exporting` phases. It automatically starts animating when entering these phases and stops when switching to the processing phase.
- **Determinate Mode**: During the `processing` phase, the progress bar switches to `determinate` mode and updates based on the ratio of completed files to the total count.
- **Completion Sync**: Ensured the progress bar reaches 100% and stops all animations upon successful completion.

#### 2. Refined Event Model & Error Semantics (`invoice_tool/gui/controller.py` & `app.py`)
- **Explicit Error Phase**: The controller now wraps exceptions into a `ProgressEvent` with an explicit `phase="error"`. This aligns the error-handling path with the standard event model used for progress updates.
- **Robust Error Handling**: The GUI's `_handle_error` method was updated to handle these structured error events, ensuring the progress bar stops animating and the status message reflects the error state accurately.
- **Reset Logic**: Added logic to explicitly stop and reset the progress bar state when starting a new processing run or when an error occurs, preventing inconsistent UI states.

### Verification Performed
- **Syntax Check**: Verified both modified files using `py_compile` to ensure no regressions were introduced.
- **Logic Review**: Confirmed the phase transitions in `app.py` correctly match the phases emitted by the backend service in `application/service.py`.
- **Code Health**: Grepped for `TODO/FIXME/HACK` in the codebase to ensure no temporary workarounds were left behind.

These minimal changes directly satisfy the F1 requirements while maintaining the existing architecture and stability approved by F2/F3/F4.

**Crafting a direct response**

I need to provide a clear and concise answer to the user. They mentioned the latest fixes, but it seems the files haven’t changed from before. I should note that we’ve gathered context through the requested analyze-mode. I’ll keep in mind to follow the structure laid out by the developer: starting with a bottom line verdict, followed by any exact remaining gaps if the response is a rejection. Let’s put this together!
F1 VERDICT: REJECT

I re-checked the plan plus the current `app.py`, `controller.py`, `service.py`, and `README.md`, and the two previously rejected compliance gaps are still present in the code as read. Tasks 1, 2, 4, 5, and 7 remain aligned with the mandatory plan requirements, but Tasks 3 and 6 are still not fully compliant on the locked progress/event requirements.

1. **Task 3 — progress/event model still does not include `error` as a phase.**  
   The plan requires a progress/event model with phase changes including `validating`, `processing`, `exporting`, `complete`, and `error` (`.sisyphus/plans/tkinter-gui-for-invoice-tool.md:224-229`).  
   Current implementation emits `validating`, `processing`, `exporting`, and `complete` through `progress_callback` in `invoice_tool/application/service.py:11-18, 29-30, 54-60`, but errors are still sent as a separate queue message in `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:164-173` rather than as an `error` phase within that model.

2. **Task 6 — locked indeterminate preflight progress semantics are still not implemented.**  
   The plan explicitly locks progress semantics to “indeterminate while preflighting/setup, determinate by input-file count during batch processing, single-step complete state for single-file mode” (`.sisyphus/plans/tkinter-gui-for-invoice-tool.md:42`).  
   In the current UI, the progress bar is still created as a plain determinate bar in `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:209-211`, and `_handle_progress()` sets the bar to `0` when `event.total == 0` instead of switching to an indeterminate mode/animation (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:280-286`). That means preflight/setup is not actually shown as indeterminate.

**What is compliant**:
- GUI exists alongside CLI, not instead of it: CLI docs remain in `README.md:38-63`.
- Tkinter GUI, picker flow, DnD file/folder support, and one-item drop rejection are present in `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:79-160`.
- Worker thread + queue + Tk `after()` polling responsiveness model is present in `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:156-173` and `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:239-278`.
- Summary and failed/conflict detail rendering are present in `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:71-91` and `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:314-382`.
- README still documents both GUI and CLI entrypoints and V1 DnD limitation in `README.md:16-44, 76-84`.

**Effort estimate**: Quick

**Why this approach**:
- I evaluated only against explicit plan requirements, especially the two retry-focus items you called out.
- The implementation is close, but final-gate approval should not waive locked requirements that are still missing in the current files.

Task ID: bg_66a461ca
Description: Fix F1 progress compliance
Duration: 3m 13s
Session ID: ses_2ffb1e46affeSZ7RPIAJd4aq6M

---

I have addressed the Final-Wave rejection from F1 by enhancing the progress bar semantics and refining the GUI event model for error handling.

### Changes Summary

#### 1. Enhanced Progress Semantics (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py`)
- **Indeterminate Mode**: The progress bar now uses `indeterminate` mode during the `validating` and `exporting` phases. It automatically starts animating when entering these phases and stops when switching to the processing phase.
- **Determinate Mode**: During the `processing` phase, the progress bar switches to `determinate` mode and updates based on the ratio of completed files to the total count.
- **Completion Sync**: Ensured the progress bar reaches 100% and stops all animations upon successful completion.

#### 2. Refined Event Model & Error Semantics (`invoice_tool/gui/controller.py` & `app.py`)
- **Explicit Error Phase**: The controller now wraps exceptions into a `ProgressEvent` with an explicit `phase="error"`. This aligns the error-handling path with the standard event model used for progress updates.
- **Robust Error Handling**: The GUI's `_handle_error` method was updated to handle these structured error events, ensuring the progress bar stops animating and the status message reflects the error state accurately.
- **Reset Logic**: Added logic to explicitly stop and reset the progress bar state when starting a new processing run or when an error occurs, preventing inconsistent UI states.

### Verification Performed
- **Syntax Check**: Verified both modified files using `py_compile` to ensure no regressions were introduced.
- **Logic Review**: Confirmed the phase transitions in `app.py` correctly match the phases emitted by the backend service in `application/service.py`.
- **Code Health**: Grepped for `TODO/FIXME/HACK` in the codebase to ensure no temporary workarounds were left behind.

These minimal changes directly satisfy the F1 requirements while maintaining the existing architecture and stability approved by F2/F3/F4.
```

I have fixed the compliance gap for F1 by ensuring the progress bar correctly demonstrates indeterminate preflight semantics from the moment processing is initiated.

### Changes Summary

- **`invoice_tool/gui/app.py`**:
    - Updated `_on_start()` to initialize the progress bar in `indeterminate` mode and start the animation immediately. This ensures that the preflight/setup phase (validating inputs) is visually represented by an animating progress bar before the first progress event is even processed.
    - Verified that `_handle_progress()` continues to manage subsequent transitions to `determinate` mode once the `processing` phase begins, and back to `indeterminate` for the `exporting` phase.
    - Confirmed that error handling and completion flows correctly stop any active animation and return the bar to a stable `determinate` state.

### Verification Results
- **Syntax Check**: Passed via `py_compile`.
- **Grep Check**: No `TODO/FIXME/HACK` found in the modified file.
- **Runtime Logic**: The change ensures deterministic visible indeterminate preflight semantics as required by the plan.

I have also recorded this finding in the project's learnings notepad to prevent future regressions regarding Tkinter progress bar initialization.

259:     def _poll_queue(self):
260:         try:
261:             while True:
262:                 msg_type, data = self.controller.event_queue.get_nowait()
263:                 if msg_type == "progress":
264:                     self._handle_progress(data)
265:                 elif msg_type == "result":
266:                     self._handle_result(data)
267:                     return # Stop polling
268:                 elif msg_type == "error":
269:                     self._handle_error(data)
270:                     return # Stop polling
271:         except tk.TclError:
272:             # Handle case where widget is destroyed during poll
273:             return
274:         except Exception:
275:             # No message in queue
276:             pass
277:         
278:         # Continue polling if not done
279:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
280:             self.after(100, self._poll_queue)
281: 
282:     def _handle_progress(self, event):
283:         self.status_var.set(event.message)
284:         
285:         # Phase-based progress semantics: indeterminate for preflight/setup, determinate for processing
286:         if event.phase in ("validating", "exporting"):
287:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'indeterminate':
288:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='indeterminate')
289:                 self.progress_bar.start(10)

291:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'determinate':
292:                 self.progress_bar.stop()
293:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
294:             
295:             if event.phase == "complete":
296:                 self.progress_var.set(100)
297:             elif event.total > 0:
298:                 self.progress_var.set((event.completed / event.total) * 100)
299:             else:
300:                 self.progress_var.set(0)

**Effort estimate**: Quick

**Why this approach**:
- The prior **progress semantics** gap is now fixed: the GUI starts in indeterminate mode at run start (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:226-230`), keeps `validating`/`exporting` indeterminate (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:285-289`), and switches to determinate percentage updates for processing/complete (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:290-300`). The backend emits the required phase sequence through the progress callback in `invoice_tool/application/service.py:11-18, 29-30, 54-60`.
- The prior **explicit error phase** gap is now fixed: worker exceptions are wrapped as `ProgressEvent(phase="error", ...)` in `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:172-179`, and the GUI handles that event in `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:325-335`.
- The rest of the required plan surface remains compliant: Tkinter GUI exists with required controls and detail panes in `invoice_tool/gui/app.py`; controller/state and result mapping exist in `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py`; README preserves CLI while documenting GUI usage and one-item DnD scope in `README.md:16-44, 76-84`.

**Concise evidence confirming Tasks 1-7 comply**:
- **Task 1**: GUI package/entrypoint exists and Tk-compatible DnD dependency is used (`invoice_tool/gui/`, `invoice_tool/gui/__main__.py`, `tkinterdnd2` import in `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:4`).
- **Task 2**: GUI-facing state and result mapping exist (`invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:13-91`).
- **Task 3**: GUI-safe adapter and event contract exist, now including explicit `error` phase wrapping (`invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:136-179`).
- **Task 4**: Required business-clean Tkinter layout, summary, and detail panes exist (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:54-211, 337-405`).
- **Task 5**: Picker flow plus single-item PDF/folder DnD rule are implemented (`invoice_tool/gui/app.py:118-160`).
- **Task 6**: Worker thread + queue + Tk `after()` polling responsiveness model is implemented, with progress/status/result/error rendering (`invoice_tool/gui/controller.py:156-179`, `invoice_tool/gui/app.py:241-335`).
- **Task 7**: README documents both GUI and CLI, plus one-item DnD limitation and V1 exclusions (`README.md:16-44, 76-84`).

**PHASE 1: READ THE CODE FIRST (before running anything)**

Do NOT run tests yet. Read the code FIRST so you know what you're testing.

1. `Bash("git diff --stat")` — see exactly which files changed. Any file outside expected scope = scope creep.
2. `Read` EVERY changed file — no exceptions, no skimming.
3. For EACH file, critically ask:
   - Does this code ACTUALLY do what the task required? (Re-read the task, compare line by line)
   - Any stubs, TODOs, placeholders, hardcoded values? (`Grep` for TODO, FIXME, HACK, xxx)
   - Logic errors? Trace the happy path AND the error path in your head.
   - Anti-patterns? (`Grep` for `as any`, `@ts-ignore`, empty catch, console.log in changed files)
   - Scope creep? Did the subagent touch things or add features NOT in the task spec?
4. Cross-check every claim:
   - Said "Updated X" — READ X. Actually updated, or just superficially touched?
   - Said "Added tests" — READ the tests. Do they test REAL behavior or just `expect(true).toBe(true)`?
   - Said "Follows patterns" — OPEN a reference file. Does it ACTUALLY match?

**If you cannot explain what every changed line does, you have NOT reviewed it.**

**PHASE 2: RUN AUTOMATED CHECKS (targeted, then broad)**

Now that you understand the code, verify mechanically:
1. `lsp_diagnostics` on EACH changed file — ZERO new errors
2. Run tests for changed modules FIRST, then full suite
3. Build/typecheck — exit 0

If Phase 1 found issues but Phase 2 passes: Phase 2 is WRONG. The code has bugs that tests don't cover. Fix the code.

**PHASE 3: HANDS-ON QA — ACTUALLY RUN IT (MANDATORY for user-facing changes)**

Tests and linters CANNOT catch: visual bugs, wrong CLI output, broken user flows, API response shape issues.

**If this task produced anything a user would SEE or INTERACT with, you MUST launch it and verify yourself.**

- **Frontend/UI**: `/playwright` skill — load the page, click through the flow, check console. Verify: page loads, interactions work, console clean, responsive.
- **TUI/CLI**: `interactive_bash` — run the command, try good input, try bad input, try --help. Verify: command runs, output correct, error messages helpful, edge inputs handled.
- **API/Backend**: `Bash` with curl — hit the endpoint, check response body, send malformed input. Verify: returns 200, body correct, error cases return proper errors.
- **Config/Build**: Actually start the service or import the config. Verify: loads without error, backward compatible.

This is NOT optional "if applicable". If the deliverable is user-facing and you did not run it, you are shipping untested work.

132:     def _on_drop(self, event):
133:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
134:             return
135:         # tkinterdnd2 can return multiple files as a brace-delimited string
136:         # if they contain spaces. On Windows, backslashes might be doubled or escaped.
137:         # We use a regex to correctly split the tcl list string.
138:         data = event.data
139:         
140:         # Tcl list splitting: matches items inside {braces} or items without spaces
141:         files = re.findall(r'\{(.*?)\}|([^\s{}]+)', data)
142:         # findall with multiple groups returns a list of tuples, flatten and filter empty
143:         files = [item[0] if item[0] else item[1] for item in files]
144:         
145:         if len(files) > 1:
146:             self.status_var.set("Error: Multiple items dropped. Please drop only ONE file or folder.")
147:             return
148: 
149:         path = files[0]
150:         self._update_input_from_path(path)
151: 
152:     def _update_input_from_path(self, path):
153:         success, message = self.controller.set_input(path)

156:             self.input_mode_var.set(f"Mode: {self.controller.state.input_mode.value.upper()}")

98:         self.event_queue = queue.Queue()
99:         self._worker_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None
100: 
101:     def set_input(self, path_str: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
102:         """Validates and sets the input path in the state."""
103:         if not path_str:
104:             self.state.input_path = ""
105:             self.state.input_mode = InputMode.NONE
106:             return False, "No path provided."
107: 
108:         path = Path(path_str)
109:         if not path.exists():
110:             return False, f"Path does not exist: {path_str}"
111: 
112:         if path.is_file():
113:             if path.suffix.lower() != ".pdf":
114:                 return False, "File is not a PDF."
115:             self.state.input_path = str(path.absolute())
116:             self.state.input_mode = InputMode.FILE
117:             return True, "Valid PDF file selected."
118:         
119:         if path.is_dir():
120:             # In V1 GUI, we allow selecting any directory. 
121:             # If it has no PDFs, the backend will surface an error during processing.
122:             self.state.input_path = str(path.absolute())
123:             self.state.input_mode = InputMode.FOLDER
124:             pdf_files = list(path.glob("*.pdf"))
125:             return True, f"Folder selected ({len(pdf_files)} PDFs)."

136:     def run_pipeline_sync(self, progress_callback: Optional[Callable[[ProgressEvent], None]] = None) -> ProcessResult:
137:         """
138:         GUI-safe backend adapter running the existing processing pipeline.
139:         Currently blocking (sync) but designed so a background worker thread can just 
140:         wrap this call.

156:     def start_processing(self):
157:         """Starts the processing pipeline in a background thread."""
158:         if self._worker_thread and self._worker_thread.is_alive():
159:             return
160: 
161:         self._worker_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run_worker, daemon=True)

164:     def _run_worker(self):

167:             def _progress_callback(event: ProgressEvent):

170:             result = self.run_pipeline_sync(progress_callback=_progress_callback)

### 本次改动
- **Summary 人性化优化**
  - 增加异常高亮逻辑：当 `失败(skipped_failed)` 或 `冲突(duplicate_conflicts)` > 0 时，指标值自动切换为醒目红色样式。
  - 正常指标保持普通样式，视觉层次更清晰。

- **下方列表区域放大**
  - 将 `PanedWindow` 权重调整为：Summary : Details = **1 : 3**（原来更小）。
  - 失败/冲突两个 Text 区域高度由 `5` 提升到 **10**，字体加大到 10，阅读明显改善。

- **GUI 全面中文化（可见文案）**
  - 窗口标题、区块标题、按钮、状态文本、弹窗标题与消息、Tab 文案全部改为中文。
  - controller 返回提示文本也已中文化，确保状态栏/错误提示统一中文。

- `invoice_tool/gui/app.py`
- `invoice_tool/gui/controller.py`

106:         path_label = ttk.Label(self.input_inner, textvariable=self.input_path_var, style="CardSecondary.TLabel", wraplength=500)

114: 
115:         # Register Drop Target
116:         self.input_card.drop_target_register(DND_FILES)
117:         self.input_card.dnd_bind('<<Drop>>', self._on_drop)
118:         self.input_inner.drop_target_register(DND_FILES)
119:         self.input_inner.dnd_bind('<<Drop>>', self._on_drop)
120: 
121:     def _on_choose_file(self):
122:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
123:             return
124:         path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("PDF files", "*.pdf")])
125:         if path:
126:             self._update_input_from_path(path)
127: 
128:     def _on_choose_folder(self):
129:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
130:             return
131:         path = filedialog.askdirectory()
132:         if path:
133:             self._update_input_from_path(path)
134: 
135:     def _on_drop(self, event):
136:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
137:             return
138:         # tkinterdnd2 can return multiple files as a brace-delimited string
139:         # if they contain spaces. On Windows, backslashes might be doubled or escaped.
140:         # We use a regex to correctly split the tcl list string.
141:         data = event.data
142:         
143:         # Tcl list splitting: matches items inside {braces} or items without spaces
144:         files = re.findall(r'\{(.*?)\}|([^\s{}]+)', data)
145:         # findall with multiple groups returns a list of tuples, flatten and filter empty
146:         files = [item[0] if item[0] else item[1] for item in files]
147:         
148:         if len(files) > 1:
149:             self.status_var.set("错误：一次仅支持拖放 1 个文件或文件夹。")
150:             return
151: 
152:         path = files[0]
153:         self._update_input_from_path(path)
154: 
155:     def _update_input_from_path(self, path):
156:         success, message = self.controller.set_input(path)
157:         if success:
158:             self.input_path_var.set(self.controller.state.input_path)
159:             mode_text = "文件" if self.controller.state.input_mode.value == "file" else "文件夹"
160:             self.input_mode_var.set(f"模式：{mode_text}")
161:             self.status_var.set(message)
162:         else:
163:             self.status_var.set(f"错误：{message}")
164:             messagebox.showerror("输入无效", message)
165: 
166:     def _build_output_card(self, parent):
167:         self.output_card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
168:         self.output_card.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0, 15))
169:

171:         self.output_inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)

173:         title = ttk.Label(self.output_inner, text="输出位置", style="SectionTitle.TLabel")
174:         title.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky="w", columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
175: 
176:         self.btn_choose_output = ttk.Button(self.output_inner, text="选择输出...", command=self._on_choose_output)
177:         self.btn_choose_output.grid(row=1, column=0, sticky="w", pady=(0, 5))
178:

181:         out_label.grid(row=1, column=1, sticky="w", padx=10)
182:

184:         self.check_overwrite = ttk.Checkbutton(self.output_inner, text="允许覆盖已有文件", variable=self.overwrite_var, style="Card.TCheckbutton")
185:         self.check_overwrite.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=2, sticky="w")
186:         
187:         self.output_inner.columnconfigure(1, weight=1)
188: 
189:     def _on_choose_output(self):
190:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
191:             return
192:         path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=".xlsx", filetypes=[("Excel files", "*.xlsx")])

194:             self.controller.set_output(path)
195:             self.output_path_var.set(path)
196:             self.status_var.set("输出路径已更新。")

198:     def _build_action_area(self, parent):
199:         frame = ttk.Frame(parent)
200:         frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=(0, 10))
201: 
202:         # Start Button
203:         self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text="开始处理", style="Action.TButton", command=self._on_start)
204:         self.start_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=(0, 15))
205: 
206:         # Progress elements
207:         progress_frame = ttk.Frame(frame)
208:         progress_frame.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True)
209: 
210:         self.status_var = tk.StringVar(value="就绪")
211:         ttk.Label(progress_frame, textvariable=self.status_var, font=("Segoe UI", 9)).pack(anchor="w", pady=(0, 2))
212: 
213:         self.progress_var = tk.DoubleVar(value=0)
214:         self.progress_bar = ttk.Progressbar(progress_frame, variable=self.progress_var, maximum=100)
215:         self.progress_bar.pack(fill=tk.X)
216: 
217:     def _on_start(self):
218:         # 1. Basic validation
219:         if not self.controller.state.input_path:
220:             messagebox.showwarning("缺少输入", "请选择 PDF 文件或文件夹。")
221:             return
222:         if not self.controller.state.output_path:
223:             messagebox.showwarning("缺少输出", "请选择输出 Excel 文件。")
224:             return
225: 
226:         # 2. Sync state
227:         self.controller.state.overwrite = self.overwrite_var.get()
228: 
229:         # 3. UI transitions
230:         self._set_ui_state(AppPhase.PROCESSING)
231:         self.status_var.set("正在启动...")
232:         self.progress_bar.configure(mode='indeterminate')
233:         self.progress_bar.start(10)
234:         self.progress_var.set(0)
235:         
236:         # Clear details
237:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
238:         self.fail_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
239:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
240:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
241:         self.conflict_text.delete("1.0", tk.END)
242:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
243: 
244:         # 4. Trigger
245:         self.controller.start_processing()
246:         self.after(100, self._poll_queue)
247: 
248:     def _set_ui_state(self, phase: AppPhase):
249:         self.controller.state.phase = phase
250:         if phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
251:             self.start_btn.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
252:             self.btn_choose_file.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
253:             self.btn_choose_folder.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
254:             self.btn_choose_output.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
255:             self.check_overwrite.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
256:         else:
257:             self.start_btn.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
258:             self.btn_choose_file.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
259:             self.btn_choose_folder.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
260:             self.btn_choose_output.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
261:             self.check_overwrite.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
262: 
263:     def _poll_queue(self):
264:         try:
265:             while True:
266:                 msg_type, data = self.controller.event_queue.get_nowait()
267:                 if msg_type == "progress":
268:                     self._handle_progress(data)
269:                 elif msg_type == "result":
270:                     self._handle_result(data)
271:                     return # Stop polling
272:                 elif msg_type == "error":
273:                     self._handle_error(data)
274:                     return # Stop polling
275:         except tk.TclError:
276:             # Handle case where widget is destroyed during poll
277:             return
278:         except Exception:
279:             # No message in queue
280:             pass
281:         
282:         # Continue polling if not done
283:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
284:             self.after(100, self._poll_queue)
285: 
286:     def _handle_progress(self, event):
287:         self.status_var.set(_localize_phase_message(event.phase, event.message))
288:         
289:         # Phase-based progress semantics: indeterminate for preflight/setup, determinate for processing
290:         if event.phase in ("validating", "exporting"):
291:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'indeterminate':
292:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='indeterminate')
293:                 self.progress_bar.start(10)
294:         else:
295:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'determinate':
296:                 self.progress_bar.stop()
297:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
298:             
299:             if event.phase == "complete":
300:                 self.progress_var.set(100)
301:             elif event.total > 0:
302:                 self.progress_var.set((event.completed / event.total) * 100)
303:             else:
304:                 self.progress_var.set(0)
305: 
306:     def _handle_result(self, result):
307:         summary, details = map_process_result_to_gui_data(result)
308:         
309:         # Update metrics
310:         for key, var in self.metric_vars.items():
311:             var.set(str(getattr(summary, key)))
312:         self._refresh_summary_alerts(summary)
313:             
314:         # Update details
315:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
316:         self.fail_text.insert(tk.END, "\n".join(details.failed_files))
317:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
318:         
319:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
320:         self.conflict_text.insert(tk.END, "\n".join(details.conflict_lines))
321:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
322:         
323:         self.status_var.set("处理完成。")
324:         self.progress_bar.stop()
325:         self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
326:         self.progress_var.set(100)
327:         self._set_ui_state(AppPhase.SUCCESS)
328:         messagebox.showinfo("完成", f"成功导出 {summary.exported} 条记录：\n{result.output_path}")
329: 
330:     def _handle_error(self, event):
331:         # Stop any active animation and ensure determinate mode on error
332:         self.progress_bar.stop()
333:         self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
334:         
335:         # Support both raw strings and ProgressEvent objects for robustness
336:         message = event.message if hasattr(event, 'message') else str(event)
337:         
338:         self.status_var.set(f"错误：{message}")
339:         self._set_ui_state(AppPhase.FAILURE)
340:         messagebox.showerror("处理失败", message)
341: 
342:     def _build_summary_section(self, parent):
343:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
344:         parent.add(card, weight=1)
345:         
346:         inner = ttk.Frame(card, style="Card.TFrame", padding=15)
347:         inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
348: 
349:         title = ttk.Label(inner, text="处理汇总", style="SectionTitle.TLabel")
350:         title.pack(anchor="w", pady=(0, 10))
351: 
352:         metrics_frame = ttk.Frame(inner, style="Card.TFrame")
353:         metrics_frame.pack(fill=tk.X)
354: 
355:         self.metric_vars = {}
356:         self.metric_value_labels = {}
357:         metrics = [
358:             ("已处理", "processed"),
359:             ("已导出", "exported"),
360:             ("失败", "skipped_failed"),
361:             ("重复跳过", "skipped_duplicate"),
362:             ("冲突", "duplicate_conflicts")
363:         ]
364: 
365:         for i, (label_text, key) in enumerate(metrics):
366:             m_frame = ttk.Frame(metrics_frame, style="Card.TFrame")
367:             m_frame.grid(row=0, column=i, padx=(0, 20) if i < len(metrics)-1 else 0)
368:             
369:             ttk.Label(m_frame, text=label_text, style="MetricName.TLabel").pack(anchor="w")
370:             var = tk.StringVar(value="0")
371:             self.metric_vars[key] = var
372:             value_label = ttk.Label(m_frame, textvariable=var, style="MetricValueNormal.TLabel")
373:             value_label.pack(anchor="w")
374:             self.metric_value_labels[key] = value_label
375: 
376:         self._refresh_summary_alerts(None)
377: 
378:     def _refresh_summary_alerts(self, summary):
379:         if not hasattr(self, "metric_value_labels"):
380:             return
381:         for key, label in self.metric_value_labels.items():
382:             try:
383:                 value = int(self.metric_vars[key].get())
384:             except Exception:
385:                 value = 0
386:             is_alert = key in ("skipped_failed", "duplicate_conflicts") and value > 0
387:             label.configure(style="MetricValueAlert.TLabel" if is_alert else "MetricValueNormal.TLabel")
388: 
389:     def _build_details_section(self, parent):
390:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
391:         parent.add(card, weight=3)
392:         
393:         inner = ttk.Frame(card, style="Card.TFrame", padding=15)
394:         inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
395: 
396:         # Notebook for Failed Files / Conflicts
397:         self.notebook = ttk.Notebook(inner)
398:         self.notebook.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
399: 
400:         # Failed Files Tab
401:         fail_frame = ttk.Frame(self.notebook, padding=5)
402:         self.notebook.add(fail_frame, text="失败文件")
403:         
404:         self.fail_text = tk.Text(fail_frame, height=10, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10), 
405:                                  bg="#fafafa", fg="#d32f2f", relief="flat", borderwidth=1, state=tk.DISABLED)
406:         fail_scroll_y = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.fail_text.yview)
407:         fail_scroll_x = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.fail_text.xview)
408:         self.fail_text.configure(yscrollcommand=fail_scroll_y.set, xscrollcommand=fail_scroll_x.set)
409:         
410:         fail_scroll_y.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
411:         fail_scroll_x.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)
412:         self.fail_text.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
413: 
414:         # Conflicts Tab
415:         conflict_frame = ttk.Frame(self.notebook, padding=5)
416:         self.notebook.add(conflict_frame, text="冲突明细")
417:         
418:         self.conflict_text = tk.Text(conflict_frame, height=10, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10),
419:                                      bg="#fafafa", fg="#f57c00", relief="flat", borderwidth=1, state=tk.DISABLED)

422:         self.conflict_text.configure(yscrollcommand=conflict_scroll_y.set, xscrollcommand=conflict_scroll_x.set)
423:         
424:         conflict_scroll_y.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
425:         conflict_scroll_x.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)
426:         self.conflict_text.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
427: 
428: 
429: def main():
430:     app = InvoiceApp()
431:     app.mainloop()
432:     return 0
433: 
434: 
435: def _extract_filename_from_message(message: str) -> str:
436:     if not message:
437:         return ""
438:     m = re.search(r"Processing\s+(.*?)\.\.\.", message)
439:     if m:
440:         return m.group(1)
441:     return ""
442: 
443: 
444: def _localize_phase_message(phase: str, raw_message: str) -> str:
445:     if phase == "validating":
446:         return "正在校验输入..."
447:     if phase == "processing":
448:         file_name = _extract_filename_from_message(raw_message)
449:         return f"正在处理：{file_name}" if file_name else "正在处理发票..."
450:     if phase == "exporting":
451:         return "正在导出 Excel..."
452:     if phase == "complete":
453:         return "处理完成。"
454:     if phase == "error":
455:         return f"错误：{raw_message}" if raw_message else "处理失败。"
456:     return raw_message
457: 
458: 
459: if __name__ == "__main__":
460:     main()

- **整体视觉升级（商务风）**

  - 状态文本新增**颜色语义**：
    - 处理中：蓝色
    - 成功：绿色
    - 警示：橙色
    - 错误：红色

- **Summary 与异常反馈更醒目**
  - 指标区改为更均衡的卡片布局（列权重优化）
  - `失败` / `冲突` 非 0 时自动红色高亮（你前面提的需求保留并强化）

- **详情区域更易读**
  - 下方区域权重继续放大（Summary:Details = 1:3）
  - 失败/冲突文本框保持放大版（高度 10）
  - Notebook 标签与文本框样式更精致

- **中文界面继续保持**
  - 主界面、按钮、状态、弹窗、Tab 全中文
  - controller 返回消息也保持中文链路

- `invoice_tool/gui/app.py`（主要视觉与交互美化）

267:         self.controller.state.phase = phase
268:         if phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
269:             self.start_btn.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
270:             self.btn_choose_file.config(state=tk.DISABLED)

281:     def _poll_queue(self):
282:         try:
283:             while True:
284:                 msg_type, data = self.controller.event_queue.get_nowait()
285:                 if msg_type == "progress":
286:                     self._handle_progress(data)
287:                 elif msg_type == "result":
288:                     self._handle_result(data)
289:                     return # Stop polling
290:                 elif msg_type == "error":
291:                     self._handle_error(data)
292:                     return # Stop polling
293:         except tk.TclError:
294:             # Handle case where widget is destroyed during poll
295:             return
296:         except Exception:
297:             # No message in queue
298:             pass
299:         
300:         # Continue polling if not done
301:         if self.controller.state.phase == AppPhase.PROCESSING:
302:             self.after(100, self._poll_queue)
303: 
304:     def _handle_progress(self, event):
305:         self._set_status(_localize_phase_message(event.phase, event.message), event.phase)
306:         
307:         # Phase-based progress semantics: indeterminate for preflight/setup, determinate for processing
308:         if event.phase in ("validating", "exporting"):
309:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'indeterminate':
310:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='indeterminate')
311:                 self.progress_bar.start(10)
312:         else:
313:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'determinate':
314:                 self.progress_bar.stop()
315:                 self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
316:             
317:             if event.phase == "complete":
318:                 self.progress_var.set(100)
319:             elif event.total > 0:
320:                 self.progress_var.set((event.completed / event.total) * 100)
321:             else:
322:                 self.progress_var.set(0)
323: 
324:     def _handle_result(self, result):
325:         summary, details = map_process_result_to_gui_data(result)
326:         
327:         # Update metrics
328:         for key, var in self.metric_vars.items():
329:             var.set(str(getattr(summary, key)))
330:         self._refresh_summary_alerts(summary)
331:             
332:         # Update details
333:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
334:         self.fail_text.insert(tk.END, "\n".join(details.failed_files))
335:         self.fail_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
336:         
337:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.NORMAL)
338:         self.conflict_text.insert(tk.END, "\n".join(details.conflict_lines))
339:         self.conflict_text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
340:         
341:         self._set_status("处理完成。", "complete")
342:         self.progress_bar.stop()

344:         self.progress_var.set(100)
345:         self._set_ui_state(AppPhase.SUCCESS)
346:         messagebox.showinfo("完成", f"成功导出 {summary.exported} 条记录：\n{result.output_path}")
347: 
348:     def _handle_error(self, event):
349:         # Stop any active animation and ensure determinate mode on error
350:         self.progress_bar.stop()
351:         self.progress_bar.configure(mode='determinate')
352:         
353:         # Support both raw strings and ProgressEvent objects for robustness
354:         message = event.message if hasattr(event, 'message') else str(event)
355:         
356:         self._set_status(f"错误：{message}", "error")
357:         self._set_ui_state(AppPhase.FAILURE)
358:         messagebox.showerror("处理失败", message)
359: 
360:     def _set_status(self, text: str, phase: str = ""):
361:         self.status_var.set(text)
362:         if not hasattr(self, "status_label"):
363:             return
364:         if phase in ("processing", "validating", "exporting"):
365:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusRunning.TLabel")
366:         elif phase == "complete":
367:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusSuccess.TLabel")
368:         elif phase == "error":
369:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusError.TLabel")
370:         elif "错误" in text:
371:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusError.TLabel")
372:         elif "已更新" in text:
373:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusWarn.TLabel")
374:         else:
375:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusNeutral.TLabel")
376: 
377:     def _build_summary_section(self, parent):
378:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
379:         parent.add(card, weight=1)

417:     def _refresh_summary_alerts(self, summary):

424:                 value = 0
425:             is_alert = key in ("skipped_failed", "duplicate_conflicts") and value > 0
426:             label.configure(style="MetricValueAlert.TLabel" if is_alert else "MetricValueNormal.TLabel")
427: 
428:     def _build_details_section(self, parent):
429:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
430:         parent.add(card, weight=3)
431:         
432:         inner = ttk.Frame(card, style="Card.TFrame", padding=15)
433:         inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
434: 
435:         # Notebook for Failed Files / Conflicts
436:         self.notebook = ttk.Notebook(inner)
437:         self.notebook.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
438: 
439:         # Failed Files Tab
440:         fail_frame = ttk.Frame(self.notebook, padding=5)
441:         self.notebook.add(fail_frame, text="失败文件")
442:         
443:         self.fail_text = tk.Text(fail_frame, height=10, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10), 
444:                                  bg="#ffffff", fg="#d32f2f", relief="solid", borderwidth=1, state=tk.DISABLED)
445:         fail_scroll_y = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.fail_text.yview)
446:         fail_scroll_x = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.fail_text.xview)
447:         self.fail_text.configure(yscrollcommand=fail_scroll_y.set, xscrollcommand=fail_scroll_x.set)
448:         
449:         fail_scroll_y.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
450:         fail_scroll_x.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)
451:         self.fail_text.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
452: 
453:         # Conflicts Tab
454:         conflict_frame = ttk.Frame(self.notebook, padding=5)
455:         self.notebook.add(conflict_frame, text="冲突明细")
456:         
457:         self.conflict_text = tk.Text(conflict_frame, height=10, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10),
458:                                      bg="#ffffff", fg="#f57c00", relief="solid", borderwidth=1, state=tk.DISABLED)
459:         conflict_scroll_y = ttk.Scrollbar(conflict_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.conflict_text.yview)
460:         conflict_scroll_x = ttk.Scrollbar(conflict_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.conflict_text.xview)
461:         self.conflict_text.configure(yscrollcommand=conflict_scroll_y.set, xscrollcommand=conflict_scroll_x.set)
462:         
463:         conflict_scroll_y.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)
464:         conflict_scroll_x.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)
465:         self.conflict_text.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
466: 
467: 
468: def main():
469:     app = InvoiceApp()
470:     app.mainloop()
471:     return 0
472: 
473: 
474: def _extract_filename_from_message(message: str) -> str:
475:     if not message:
476:         return ""
477:     m = re.search(r"Processing\s+(.*?)\.\.\.", message)
478:     if m:
479:         return m.group(1)
480:     return ""
481: 
482: 
483: def _localize_phase_message(phase: str, raw_message: str) -> str:
484:     if phase == "validating":
485:         return "正在校验输入..."
486:     if phase == "processing":
487:         file_name = _extract_filename_from_message(raw_message)
488:         return f"正在处理：{file_name}" if file_name else "正在处理发票..."
489:     if phase == "exporting":
490:         return "正在导出 Excel..."
491:     if phase == "complete":
492:         return "处理完成。"
493:     if phase == "error":
494:         return f"错误：{raw_message}" if raw_message else "处理失败。"
495:     return raw_message
496: 
497: 
498: if __name__ == "__main__":
499:     main()

(End of file - total 499 lines)
</content>
```

## Assistant (Hephaestus (Deep Agent) · gpt-5.3-codex · 16.3s)

已全部修好，你提的 3 个问题都落地了 ✅

### 1) 处理汇总默认高度不够（已修）
我做了两层修复：
- 窗口默认尺寸增大：`1080x840`（最小 `900x640`）
- 启动后自动设置 `PanedWindow` 分割位置（延迟重试机制），默认把上半汇总区抬高到更安全高度  
  - 实测启动后 `sash=220`，不会再默认挤压汇总数字显示

### 2) 失败文件 / 冲突明细 页签选中态反了（已修）
- 给 `TNotebook.Tab` 增加了明确状态映射：
  - **selected**：蓝底白字（清晰高亮）
  - **active hover**：浅蓝底深蓝字
  - **非选中**：灰底深灰字
- 这样视觉上不会“像反选”，当前页签会非常明确。

### 3) 下方列表再加高，并默认多显示几列文本（已修）
- 两个文本区从之前基础上再次扩大为：
  - `height=14`
  - `width=145`
- 失败文件与冲突明细都同步放大，默认可见行和可见列都更多，横向阅读压力更小。

## Assistant (Hephaestus (Deep Agent) · gpt-5.3-codex · 13.5s)

高级美化这三项我已经全部做完并验证通过 ✅

### 你要求的 3 个增强，已落地

- **Summary 改成统计卡片块**
  - 五个指标都改成卡片化展示（浅底色 + 图标符号 + 大数字）
  - 异常项（失败、冲突）仍会自动高亮，颜色更醒目
  - 信息层级从“表格感”变成“仪表盘感”

- **输入/输出区加分组边框标题条**
  - 输入区改为 `LabelFrame`：`输入来源`
  - 输出区改为 `LabelFrame`：`输出位置`
  - 视觉上更像“业务表单分组”，一眼能区分区域职责

- **进度区增加“当前阶段 + 百分比”双显示**
  - 新增两条实时文本：
    - `当前阶段：...`
    - `进度：...`
  - 处理阶段会同步更新（例如处理中 37%）
  - 预处理/导出阶段也有明确阶段显示（百分比可用 `--`）

---

- `invoice_tool/gui/app.py`

311:     def _poll_queue(self):
312:         try:
313:             while True:
314:                 msg_type, data = self.controller.event_queue.get_nowait()
315:                 if msg_type == "progress":
316:                     self._handle_progress(data)
317:                 elif msg_type == "result":
318:                     self._handle_result(data)
319:                     return # Stop polling
320:                 elif msg_type == "error":

326:         except Exception:

335:         self._set_status(_localize_phase_message(event.phase, event.message), event.phase)

338:         if event.phase in ("validating", "exporting"):
339:             if self.progress_bar['mode'] != 'indeterminate':

401:             "processing": "处理中",

410:     def _set_status(self, text: str, phase: str = ""):
411:         self.status_var.set(text)
412:         if not hasattr(self, "status_label"):
413:             return
414:         if phase in ("processing", "validating", "exporting"):
415:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusRunning.TLabel")

418:         elif phase == "error":

420:         elif "错误" in text:
421:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusError.TLabel")
422:         elif "已更新" in text:
423:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusWarn.TLabel")
424:         else:
425:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusNeutral.TLabel")
426: 
427:     def _build_summary_section(self, parent):
428:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
429:         parent.add(card, weight=1)

461:

466: 
467:     def _refresh_summary_alerts(self, summary):
468:         if not hasattr(self, "metric_value_labels"):
469:             return

472:             try:

525: def _extract_filename_from_message(message: str) -> str:
526:     if not message:
527:         return ""
528:     m = re.search(r"Processing\s+(.*?)\.\.\.", message)
529:     if m:
530:         return m.group(1)
531:     return ""
532: 
533: 
534: def _localize_phase_message(phase: str, raw_message: str) -> str:
535:     if phase == "validating":
536:         return "正在校验输入..."
537:     if phase == "processing":
538:         file_name = _extract_filename_from_message(raw_message)
539:         return f"正在处理：{file_name}" if file_name else "正在处理发票..."
540:     if phase == "exporting":
541:         return "正在导出 Excel..."
542:     if phase == "complete":
543:         return "处理完成。"
544:     if phase == "error":
545:         return f"错误：{raw_message}" if raw_message else "处理失败。"
546:     return raw_message

405:             "": "待命",
406:         }
407:         self.phase_var.set(f"当前阶段：{phase_map.get(phase, phase)}")
408:         self.percent_var.set(f"进度：{percent_text}")
409: 
410:     def _set_status(self, text: str, phase: str = ""):
411:         self.status_var.set(text)
412:         if not hasattr(self, "status_label"):
413:             return
414:         if phase in ("processing", "validating", "exporting"):
415:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusRunning.TLabel")
416:         elif phase == "complete":
417:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusSuccess.TLabel")
418:         elif phase == "error":
419:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusError.TLabel")
420:         elif "错误" in text:
421:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusError.TLabel")
422:         elif "已更新" in text:
423:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusWarn.TLabel")
424:         else:
425:             self.status_label.configure(style="StatusNeutral.TLabel")
426: 
427:     def _build_summary_section(self, parent):
428:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
429:         parent.add(card, weight=1)
430:         
431:         inner = ttk.Frame(card, style="Card.TFrame", padding=15)
432:         inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
433: 
434:         title = ttk.Label(inner, text="处理汇总", style="SectionTitle.TLabel")
435:         title.pack(anchor="w", pady=(0, 10))
436: 
437:         metrics_frame = ttk.Frame(inner, style="Card.TFrame")
438:         metrics_frame.pack(fill=tk.X)
439: 
440:         self.metric_vars = {}
441:         self.metric_value_labels = {}
442:         metrics = [
443:             ("📄", "已处理", "processed", "#eaf2ff", "#1e40af", "#1e40af"),
444:             ("✅", "已导出", "exported", "#e8f8ef", "#166534", "#166534"),
445:             ("⚠", "失败", "skipped_failed", "#fff1f2", "#9f1239", "#dc2626"),
446:             ("↺", "重复跳过", "skipped_duplicate", "#fff7e6", "#92400e", "#92400e"),
447:             ("‼", "冲突", "duplicate_conflicts", "#fff4e5", "#9a3412", "#ea580c")
448:         ]
449: 
450:         for i, (icon, label_text, key, bg, normal_fg, alert_fg) in enumerate(metrics):
451:             m_frame = tk.Frame(metrics_frame, bg=bg, bd=1, relief="solid", padx=10, pady=8)
452:             m_frame.grid(row=0, column=i, padx=(0, 16) if i < len(metrics)-1 else 0, sticky="nsew")
453: 
454:             tk.Label(m_frame, text=icon, bg=bg, fg=normal_fg, font=("Segoe UI", 11, "bold")).pack(anchor="w")
455:             tk.Label(m_frame, text=label_text, bg=bg, fg=self.text_secondary, font=("Segoe UI", 9)).pack(anchor="w")
456:             var = tk.StringVar(value="0")
457:             self.metric_vars[key] = var
458:             value_label = tk.Label(m_frame, textvariable=var, bg=bg, fg=normal_fg, font=("Segoe UI", 16, "bold"))
459:             value_label.pack(anchor="w")
460:             self.metric_value_labels[key] = (value_label, normal_fg, alert_fg)
461: 
462:         for i in range(len(metrics)):
463:             metrics_frame.columnconfigure(i, weight=1)
464: 
465:         self._refresh_summary_alerts(None)
466: 
467:     def _refresh_summary_alerts(self, summary):
468:         if not hasattr(self, "metric_value_labels"):
469:             return
470:         for key, label_pack in self.metric_value_labels.items():
471:             label, normal_fg, alert_fg = label_pack
472:             try:
473:                 value = int(self.metric_vars[key].get())
474:             except Exception:
475:                 value = 0
476:             is_alert = key in ("skipped_failed", "duplicate_conflicts") and value > 0
477:             label.configure(fg=alert_fg if is_alert else normal_fg)
478: 
479:     def _build_details_section(self, parent):
480:         card = ttk.Frame(parent, style="Card.TFrame")
481:         parent.add(card, weight=4)
482:         
483:         inner = ttk.Frame(card, style="Card.TFrame", padding=15)
484:         inner.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
485: 
486:         # Notebook for Failed Files / Conflicts
487:         self.notebook = ttk.Notebook(inner)
488:         self.notebook.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)
489: 
490:         # Failed Files Tab
491:         fail_frame = ttk.Frame(self.notebook, padding=5)
492:         self.notebook.add(fail_frame, text="失败文件")
493:         
494:         self.fail_text = tk.Text(fail_frame, height=20, width=145, wrap=tk.NONE, font=("Consolas", 10), 
495:                                  bg="#ffffff", fg="#d32f2f", relief="solid", borderwidth=1, state=tk.DISABLED)
496:         fail_scroll_y = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.fail_text.yview)
497:         fail_scroll_x = ttk.Scrollbar(fail_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.fail_text.xview)
498:         self.fail_text.configure(yscrollcommand=fail_scroll_y.set, xscrollcommand=fail_scroll_x.set)
499:

519: def main():
520:     app = InvoiceApp()
521:     app.mainloop()

524: 
525: def _extract_filename_from_message(message: str) -> str:
526:     if not message:
527:         return ""
528:     m = re.search(r"Processing\s+(.*?)\.\.\.", message)
529:     if m:
530:         return m.group(1)
531:     return ""
532: 
533: 
534: def _localize_phase_message(phase: str, raw_message: str) -> str:
535:     if phase == "validating":
536:         return "正在校验输入..."
537:     if phase == "processing":
538:         file_name = _extract_filename_from_message(raw_message)
539:         return f"正在处理：{file_name}" if file_name else "正在处理发票..."
540:     if phase == "exporting":
541:         return "正在导出 Excel..."
542:     if phase == "complete":
543:         return "处理完成。"
544:     if phase == "error":
545:         return f"错误：{raw_message}" if raw_message else "处理失败。"
546:     return raw_message

### 本轮新增
- **统计卡片再美化**

  - 数字与图标层级更清晰

  - 待命：`开始处理`
  - 处理中：`处理中...`

  - 默认：`失败文件 (0)` / `冲突明细 (0)`
  - 结果出来后自动更新数量（例如 `(3)`、`(5)`）
  - 新一轮开始会清零再计数

- **列表区进一步加大**
  - 失败/冲突两个文本区统一到更大尺寸：`height=20, width=150`

## Assistant (Hephaestus (Deep Agent) · gpt-5.3-codex · 24.0s)

这个问题已经修好了 ✅

我给“失败文件 / 冲突明细”做了**独立 Tab 样式**，不再用通用 `TNotebook.Tab`，避免状态映射造成的“选中看起来缩小”错觉。现在行为是：

- **选中态**：更大、更稳、更明显（粗体、padding 更大、蓝底白字）
- **未选中态**：稍小、次级视觉（普通字重、padding 略小）
- 不会再出现你说的“选中像缩放、未选中反而放大”的反差

### 修改文件
- `invoice_tool/gui/app.py`

### 关键验证
- `python -m py_compile invoice_tool/gui/app.py` ✅
- 样式检查确认：
  - `notebook_style = Detail.TNotebook`
  - `selected_font = Segoe UI 10 bold`
  - `selected_padding = (14, 9)`
  - `normal_font = Segoe UI 9`
  - `normal_padding = (12, 6)` ✅

**Choosing safe ASCII/unicode symbols**

我发现一个兼容性点：Windows 当前终端编码（GBK）对彩色 emoji 圆点不稳定，导致输出验证报编码错。  
我改成**兼容符号状态点**（`●/○`），同时保留“失败/冲突”语义区分，这样 UI 稳定且不会乱码。随后我再跑一次验证。

### 改动结果
- 失败文件 Tab：`● 失败文件 (n)` / `○ 失败文件 (0)`
- 冲突明细 Tab：`◆ 冲突明细 (n)` / `◇ 冲突明细 (0)`

### 行为逻辑

- 我最初用了 emoji 彩色点，但你这个 Windows 终端编码（GBK）下验证会报编码错。
